statement\r\nStudent track\r\nProfessional track\r\nNASSCOM Logo\r\nAutomating Test Case Generation with AI\r\nDevelop an AI-powered system that automatically converts healthcare software requirements into compliant, traceable test cases integrated with enterprise toolchains.\r\n\r\nChallenge\r\nHealthcare software development is constrained by complex regulatory requirements, diverse data formats, and the heavy burden of manual test c reation. QA teams spend enormous time converting specifications into test cases, ensuring compliance, and maintaining traceability across tools. This slows product cycles and limits scalability in a highly regulated domain where precision and compliance are critical.\r\n\r\nObjective\r\nBuild an AI-powered system that autonomously generates test cases from requirements and specifications, reducing manual testing effort while ensuring compliance, scalability, and integration with existing enterprise toolchains.\r\n\r\nSolution Capabilities:\r\nAutomate Test Case Generation:Convert natural language and structured specifications into test cases and datasets across multiple formats (PDF, Word, XML, Markup).\r\nUnderstand Complex Requirements:Accurately interpret healthcare-specific regulations and domain-heavy specifications.\r\nIntegrate with Toolchains:Seamlessly connect with ALM platforms such as Jira, Polarion, and Azure DevOps.\r\nEnsure Compliance & Traceability:Support FDA, IEC 62304, ISO 9001, ISO 13485, and ISO 27001 standards with full requirement-to-test traceability.\r\nEnable GDPR-Compliant Pilots:Provide readiness for GDPR-compliant Proof of Concepts (PoCs) to demonstrate solution scalability.\r\nTech Stack:Use of Google AI technologies (Gemini, Vertex AI, BigQuery, Firebase, Agent Builder).\r\n\r\nView less\r\nJKCement Logo\r\nOptimizing Cement Operations with Generative AI\r\nCreate a Generative AI–driven platform for autonomous cement plant operations that optimizes energy use, quality, and sustainability across processes.\r\n\r\nChallenge\r\nCement plants are among the most energy-intensive industries in India, with complex, interlinked processes that demand constant balancing. Variability in raw material, grinding inefficiencies, high-temperature clinkerization, and siloed control systems often lead to wasted energy, inconsistent product quality, and higher environmental impact. Meanwhile, the industry faces urgent pressure to integrate alternative fuels, improve thermal substitution rates, and operate sustainably at scale.\r\n\r\nObjective\r\nBuild a Generative AI–powered platform for autonomous plant operations and cross-process optimization. The solution should reduce energy consumption, improve product quality, stabilize production, and accelerate sustainability through intelligent control and decision-making.\r\n\r\nSolution Capabilities:\r\nOptimize Raw Materials & Grinding:Ingest real-time feed data to predict variability, fine-tune grinding efficiency, and minimize energy losses.\r\nBalance Clinkerization Parameters:Continuously monitor high-temperature operations, adjusting controls to lower energy demand while reducing environmental impact.\r\nEnsure Quality Consistency:Use Generative AI to detect fluctuations in inputs and provide proactive quality corrections.\r\nMaximize Alternative Fuel Use:Model diverse fuel combinations, optimize thermal substitution rates, and reduce reliance on fossil fuels.\r\nEnable Strategic Cross-Process Optimization:Fuse siloed data streams (raw material → clinker → utilities) into a unified AI layer for holistic decision-making.\r\nEnhance Plant Utilities & Material Handling:Predict and minimize energy consumption in utilities and optimize internal logistics flows.\r\nTech Stack:Use of Google AI technologies (Gemini, Vertex AI, Cloud Vision, BigQuery, Firebase, Agent Builder).\r\n\r\nView less\r\nLVX Logo\r\nAI Analyst for Startup Evaluation\r\nBuild an AI-powered analyst platform that evaluates startups by synthesizing founder materials and public data to generate concise, actionable investment insights.\r\n\r\nChallenge\r\nEarly-stage investors often drown in unstructured startup data — pitch decks, founder calls, emails, and scattered news reports. Traditional analysis is time-consuming, inconsistent, and prone to missing red flags. What’s needed is an AI analyst that can cut through the noise, evaluate startups like a trained associate, and generate investor-ready insights at scale.\r\n\r\nObjective\r\nBuild an AI-powered analyst that reviews founder material and public data to create concise, actionable deal notes with clear benchmarks and risk assessments across sectors and geographies.\r\n\r\nSolution Capabilities:\r\nIngest pitch decks, call transcripts, founder updates, and emails to generate structured deal notes.\r\nBenchmark startups against sector peers using financial multiples, hiring data, and traction signals.\r\nFlag potential risk indicators like inconsistent metrics, inflated market size, or unusual churn patterns.\r\nSummary growth potential and generate investor-ready recommendations tailored to customizable weightages.\r\nTech Stack:Use of Google AI technologies (Gemini, Vertex AI, Cloud Vision, BigQuery, Firebase, Agent Builder).\r\n\r\nView less\r\nLVX Logo\r\nPersonalized Trip Planner with AI\r\nDevelop an AI-powered personalized trip planner that dynamically creates end-to-end itineraries tailored to individual budgets, interests, and real-time conditions with seamless booking capabilities.\r\n\r\nChallenge\r\nTravelers often struggle to create itineraries that balance budget, time, and personal interests. Existing tools provide generic suggestions, but they rarely adapt to individual preferences like cultural heritage, nightlife, or adventure. This leaves users spending hours piecing together trips from scattered sources, often missing hidden gems or overspending.\r\n\r\nObjective\r\nBuild an AI-powered trip planner that generates personalized, end-to-end itineraries tailored to a traveler’s budget, interests, and available time. The solution should simplify trip planning and deliver adaptive recommendations in real time. Once finalized, the traveller should get the final itinerary and the system should also book it through EMT inventory in just click of a button and accept payment.\r\n\r\nSolution Capabilities:\r\nGenerate dynamic itineraries that adapt to user inputs on budget, trip duration, and themes (heritage, nightlife, adventure, etc.).\r\n Aggregate data from multiple sources (maps, events, local guides) to recommendaccommodation, transport, and experiences.\r\nProvide multilingual, interactive interfaces for personalized travel assistance across regions in India.  \r\nOffer  smart adjustments in real time (e.g., weather changes, delays, or last-minute bookings).\r\nDeliver a shareable, optimized itinerary with cost breakdowns and book the tickets in a click of a button after accepting payment.\r\nTech Stack:Use of Google AI technologies (Gemini, Vertex AI, Maps API, Firebase, BigQuery).\r\n\r\nView less\r\nMore Problem statements will be released soon. Stay tuned for updates.\r\nOur partners\r\nProblem statement partners\r\n\r\nEcosystem partner\r\n\r\nTimeline\r\ntimeline desktop\r\nRequirements\r\nWhat to submit\r\nClear proposal\r\nSubmit a compelling vision for your AI solution, highlighting its positive impact and alignment with one of the focus areas.\r\nClearly articulate the problem your solution addresses and how it will benefit the community.\r\nDemonstrate the feasibility of your project and its potential for scalability.\r\nFunctional prototype\r\nBuild a working prototype using Google Cloud's AI tools.\r\nEnsure the prototype effectively demonstrates your solution's capabilities and benefits.\r\nComprehensive documentation\r\nProvide detailed instructions for judges to access and test your solution.\r\nInclude a link to a public YouTube or Vimeo video (3 minutes) showcasing your AI creation in action.\r\nSubmit a text description explaining your project's goals, functionalities, technical implementation, and social impact.\r\nCategory specification\r\nClearly identify the focus area you are submitting for.\r\nSubmission specifics\r\nFunctionality\r\nYour project must be functional and demonstrate a clear solution to the chosen social challenge. Steps 6–10 are optional for extra GCP usage and Cloud Run deploy.\n\n**Phase 1: Project + Billing**\n- Create/select project\n  - Console: IAM & Admin → Manage resources → Create project → note `PROJECT_ID`.\n  - CLI: `gcloud projects create <PROJECT_ID>` (if you prefer CLI).\n- Link billing\n  - Console: Billing → Link billing account → choose your billing account.\n  - Reason: Vertex AI, Cloud Run, and Maps require a billed project; your free credits apply here.\n\n**Phase 2: Enable Required APIs**\n- Vertex AI, Cloud Run, Cloud Build, Artifact Registry, Secret Manager, BigQuery, Firestore\n  - CLI: `gcloud services enable aiplatform.googleapis.com run.googleapis.com cloudbuild.googleapis.com artifactregistry.googleapis.com secretmanager.googleapis.com bigquery.googleapis.com firestore.googleapis.com`\n- Maps Places API (Maps Platform)\n  - Console: APIs & Services → Library → search “Places API” → Enable.\n  - Optional CLI: `gcloud services enable places-backend.googleapis.com`\n- Set active project and auth\n  - `gcloud config set project <PROJECT_ID>`\n  - `gcloud auth login`\n  - `gcloud auth application-default login`\n\n**Phase 3: Vertex AI Region**\n- Use `us-central1` (Gemini 1.5 Flash is available; cost‑efficient).\n- Note env var: `GCP_LOCATION=us-central1`.\n\n**Phase 4: Maps API Key**\n- Create key\n  - Console: APIs & Services → Credentials → Create credentials → API key.\n- Restrict key\n  - API restrictions: limit to “Places API” only.\n  - Application restrictions: None for prototype (Cloud Run has dynamic IPs). Tighten later if needed.\n- Note env var: `MAPS_API_KEY=<YOUR_KEY>`.\n- Set a daily quota cap (optional but recommended): APIs & Services → Quotas → Places API.\n\n**Phase 5: Budgets and Alerts**\n- Console: Billing → Budgets & alerts → Create budget for this project.\n- Set thresholds: 10%, 25%, 50% email alerts.\n- Maps Platform: ensure $200/month free credit is active (shown in Maps Console).\n\nStop here and you can run locally with Vertex + Maps.\n\n**Phase 6 (Optional): Firestore (save itineraries)**\n- Create Firestore (Native mode)\n  - Console: Firestore → Select Native mode → Choose location (e.g., nam5 or asia-south1).\n- IAM for runtime (later with Cloud Run)\n  - Ensure the Cloud Run service account has `roles/datastore.user`.\n\n**Phase 7 (Optional): BigQuery (usage logging)**\n- Create dataset (US multi‑region to match Gemini)\n  - `bq --location=US mk -d trip_planner`\n- IAM for runtime\n  - Grant service account `roles/bigquery.dataEditor` on the dataset.\n\n**Phase 8 (Optional): Secret Manager**\n- Store Maps key\n  - Console: Security → Secret Manager → Create secret `MAPS_API_KEY`.\n- IAM\n  - Grant Cloud Run service account `roles/secretmanager.secretAccessor`.\n\n**Phase 9 (Optional): Prepare Cloud Run Deploy**\n- Enable APIs already covered in Phase 2.\n- Artifact Registry repo (optional; gcloud build can create on push)\n  - Example: `gcloud artifacts repositories create containers --repository-format=docker --location=us --description=\"Trip Planner\"`\n- Service account (optional; you can use the default compute SA)\n  - Grant minimal roles: `roles/aiplatform.user`, plus optional roles from Phases 6–8.\n\n**Phase 10 (Deploy later)**\n- Build and deploy (example; I’ll provide Dockerfile and app)\n  - `gcloud builds submit --tag gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/trip-planner`\n  - `gcloud run deploy trip-planner --image gcr.io/$PROJECT_ID/trip-planner --region us-central1 --allow-unauthenticated`\n- Set env vars on Cloud Run\n  - `GCP_PROJECT_ID`, `GCP_LOCATION=us-central1`, and either `MAPS_API_KEY` or attach the Secret.\n\n**What to share back so I can wire the prototype**\n- `PROJECT_ID`\n- `GCP_LOCATION=us-central1`\n- `MAPS_API_KEY` (or confirm you’ll store in Secret Manager)\n- Whether to enable Firestore/BigQuery in prototype now or keep optional\n\nIf you want, we can go step‑by‑step interactively: tell me when Step 1–5 are done, and I’ll start scaffolding and hand you a runnable app."}]}
